# 2024 - 2025 Yuan Ze University Academic Calendar

March 13, 2024, Approved by the 14th Executive Council Meeting of the 2024 Academic Year; March 25, 2024 Filed for Referenced by the Ministry of Education via official letter Tai Jiao Gao (1) Zi No. 1130032094; July 10, 2024, Amended and Approved by the 22nd Executive Council Meeting of the 2024 Academic Year; September 11, 2024, Amended and Approved by the 2nd Executive Council Meeting of the 2024 Academic Year; December 18, 2024, Amended and Approved by the 8th Executive Council Meeting of the 2024 Academic Year
